   "cell_type": "code",
   "source": [
    "# Calculate correlations to identify highly correlated metrics\n",
    "correlation_matrix = df.corr()\n",
    "\n",
    "# Select target metrics for prediction\n",
    "new_target_metrics = ['GMV ARR (Cr)', 'NMV ARR (INR Cr)', 'EBITDA Margin %']\n",
    "\n",
    "# Find highly correlated features for each target metric\n",
    "selected_features = []\n",
    "for target in new_target_metrics:\n",
    "    correlations = correlation_matrix[target].sort_values(ascending=False)\n",
    "    # Exclude the target itself and pick the top 3 highly correlated features\n",
    "    top_features = correlations.index[1:4].tolist()\n",
    "    selected_features.extend(top_features)\n",
    "\n",
    "# Remove duplicates from selected features\n",
    "selected_features = list(set(selected_features))\n",
    "\n",
    "# Display selected features and target metrics\n",
    "print(\"Selected Features:\", selected_features)\n",
    "print(\"Target Metrics:\", new_target_metrics)"
   ],
   "id": "12711d5ba6597e21",

    {
     "name": "stdout",

     "text": [
      "Selected Features: ['Targeted ROAS', 'Gross Margin ARR (INR Cr)', 'Cash-in Revenue', 'MRR (L)', 'Contribution Margin 2 %', 'Revenues per week (L)', 'NMV MRR (L)', 'ON Platform - Organic', 'Overall Marketing spend / week (L)']\n",
      "Target Metrics: ['GMV ARR (Cr)', 'NMV ARR (INR Cr)', 'EBITDA Margin %']\n"
     ]
    }
   ],

   "cell_type": "code",
   "source": [
    "\n",
    "X = df[selected_features].values[:-1]\n",
    "y = df[new_target_metrics].values[1:]\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "models = {}\n",
    "for i, target in enumerate(new_target_metrics):\n",
    "    model = LinearRegression()\n",
    "    model.fit(X, y[:, i])\n",
    "    models[target] = model\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "last_known = df[selected_features].iloc[-1].values.reshape(1, -1)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "future_predictions = []\n",
    "current_features = last_known\n",
    "\n",
    "for _ in range(10):\n",
    "    next_prediction = []\n",
    "    for target in new_target_metrics:\n",
    "        pred = models[target].predict(current_features)[0]\n",
    "        next_prediction.append(pred)\n",
    "    future_predictions.append(next_prediction)\n",
    "    \n",
    "   \n",
    "    current_features = current_features * 1.02  # Assuming 2% growth rate\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "future_years = [f\"FY{i+1}\" for i in range(10)]\n",
    "predictions_df = pd.DataFrame(future_predictions, \n",
    "                            columns=new_target_metrics,\n",
    "                            index=future_years)\n",
    "\n",
    "plt.figure(figsize=(15, 8))\n",
    "for metric in new_target_metrics:\n",
    "    plt.plot(future_years, predictions_df[metric], marker='o', label=metric)\n",
    "\n",
    "plt.title('10-Year Financial Metrics Forecast (Enhanced Model)')\n",
    "plt.xlabel('Fiscal Year')\n",
    "plt.ylabel('Value')\n",
    "plt.legend()\n",
    "plt.xticks(rotation=45)\n",
    "plt.grid(True)\n",
    "plt.tight_layout()\n",
    "plt.show()\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "print(\"\\\n",
    "Predicted Values for Next 10 Fiscal Years:\")\n",
    "print(predictions_df.round(2))\n",
    "\n",
    "print(\"\\\n",
    "Feature Importance:\")\n",
    "for target in new_target_metrics:\n",
    "    coefficients = pd.Series(models[target].coef_, index=selected_features)\n",
    "    print(f\"\\\n",
    "{target}:\")\n",
    "    print(coefficients.sort_values(ascending=False).round(4))\n",
    "    print(coefficients.sort_values(ascending=False).round(4))"
   ],

   "source": [
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "X = df[selected_features].values[:-1]\n",
    "y = df[new_target_metrics].values[1:]\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "scaler = StandardScaler()\n",
    "X_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(X)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(X_scaled, y, test_size=0.2, random_state=42)\n",
    "\n",
    "models = {\n",
    "    'Linear Regression': LinearRegression(),\n",
    "    'Random Forest': RandomForestRegressor(n_estimators=100, random_state=42),\n",
    "    'Gradient Boosting': GradientBoostingRegressor(random_state=42),\n",
    "    'XGBoost': XGBRegressor(random_state=42)\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "results = {}\n",
    "\n",
    "for target_idx, target in enumerate(new_target_metrics):\n",
    "    print(f\"\\\n",
    "Results for {target}:\")\n",
    "    print(\"-\" * 50)\n",
    "    \n",
    "    target_results = {}\n",
    "    for model_name, model in models.items():\n",
    "    \n",
    "        model.fit(X_train, y_train[:, target_idx])\n",
    "     \n",
    "        y_pred = model.predict(X_test)\n",
    "        if len(y_pred.shape) > 1:\n",
    "            y_pred = y_pred[:, target_idx]\n",
    "            \n",
    "      \n",
    "        r2 = r2_score(y_test[:, target_idx], y_pred)\n",
    "        mae = mean_absolute_error(y_test[:, target_idx], y_pred)\n",
    "        rmse = np.sqrt(mean_squared_error(y_test[:, target_idx], y_pred))\n",
    "        \n",
    "      \n",
    "        target_results[model_name] = {\n",
    "            'R2': r2,\n",
    "            'MAE': mae,\n",
    "            'RMSE': rmse\n",
    "        }\n",
    "        \n",
    "        print(f\"\\\n",
    "{model_name}:\")\n",
    "        print(f\"R2 Score: {r2:.4f}\")\n",
    "        print(f\"MAE: {mae:.4f}\")\n",
    "        print(f\"RMSE: {rmse:.4f}\")\n",
    "    \n",
    "    results[target] = target_results\n",
    "\n",
    "best_models = {}\n",
    "for target in new_target_metrics:\n",
    "    best_r2 = -float('inf')\n",
    "    best_model = None\n",
    "    for model_name in models.keys():\n",
    "        r2 = results[target][model_name]['R2']\n",
    "        if r2 > best_r2:\n",
    "            best_r2 = r2\n",
    "            best_model = model_name\n",
    "    best_models[target] = best_model\n",
    "\n",
    "print(\"\\\n",
    "Best Models:\")\n",
    "for target, model in best_models.items():\n",
    "    print(f\"{target}: {model}\")\n",
    "\n",
    "future_predictions = []\n",
    "current_features = scaler.transform(df[selected_features].iloc[-1:].values)\n",
    "\n",
    "for _ in range(10):\n",
    "    next_prediction = []\n",
    "    for target_idx, target in enumerate(new_target_metrics):\n",
    "        best_model_name = best_models[target]\n",
    "        model = models[best_model_name]\n",
    "        pred = model.predict(current_features)[0]\n",
    "        next_prediction.append(pred)\n",
    "    future_predictions.append(next_prediction)\n",
    "    current_features = current_features * 1.02\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "future_years = [f\"FY{i+1}\" for i in range(10)]\n",
    "predictions_df = pd.DataFrame(future_predictions, \n",
    "                            columns=new_target_metrics,\n",
    "                            index=future_years)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "plt.figure(figsize=(15, 8))\n",
    "for metric in new_target_metrics:\n",
    "    plt.plot(future_years, predictions_df[metric], marker='o', label=metric)\n",
    "\n",
    "plt.title('10-Year Financial Metrics Forecast (Best Models)')\n",
    "plt.xlabel('Fiscal Year')\n",
    "plt.ylabel('Value')\n",
    "plt.legend()\n",
    "plt.xticks(rotation=45)\n",
    "plt.grid(True)\n",
    "plt.tight_layout()\n",
    "plt.show()\n",
    "\n",
    "print(\"\\\n",
    "Updated Predictions using Best Models:\")\n",
    "print(predictions_df.round(2))"

    "\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "df = pd.read_csv('r_data2.csv')\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "selected_features = ['Targeted Website Conversion', 'Average Order Value', 'Targeted ROAS', \n",
    "                    'ON Platform - Organic', 'ON Platform - Paid', '3rd Party Channels',\n",
    "                    'Net # of orders / day', 'Revenues per week (L)', 'MRR (L)']\n",
    "\n",
    "new_target_metrics = ['GMV ARR (Cr)', 'NMV ARR (INR Cr)', 'EBITDA Margin %']\n",
    "\n",
    "X = df[selected_features].values[:-1]\n",
    "y = df[new_target_metrics].values[1:]\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "scaler = StandardScaler()\n",
    "X_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(X)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(X_scaled, y, test_size=0.2, random_state=42)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "models = {\n",
    "    'Linear Regression': LinearRegression(),\n",
    "    'Random Forest': RandomForestRegressor(n_estimators=100, random_state=42),\n",
    "    'Gradient Boosting': GradientBoostingRegressor(random_state=42),\n",
    "    'XGBoost': XGBRegressor(random_state=42)\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "results = {}\n",
    "\n",
    "for target_idx, target in enumerate(new_target_metrics):\n",
    "    print(f\"\\\n",
    "Results for {target}:\")\n",
    "    print(\"-\" * 50)\n",
    "    \n",
    "    target_results = {}\n",
    "    for model_name, model in models.items():\n",
    "        \n",
    "        model.fit(X_train, y_train[:, target_idx])\n",
    "        \n",
    "        \n",
    "        y_pred = model.predict(X_test)\n",
    "        if len(y_pred.shape) > 1:\n",
    "            y_pred = y_pred[:, target_idx]\n",
    "            \n",
    "        \n",
    "        r2 = r2_score(y_test[:, target_idx], y_pred)\n",
    "        mae = mean_absolute_error(y_test[:, target_idx], y_pred)\n",
    "        rmse = np.sqrt(mean_squared_error(y_test[:, target_idx], y_pred))\n",
    "        \n",
    "        \n",
    "        target_results[model_name] = {\n",
    "            'R2': r2,\n",
    "            'MAE': mae,\n",
    "            'RMSE': rmse\n",
    "        }\n",
    "        \n",
    "        print(f\"\\\n",
    "{model_name}:\")\n",
    "        print(f\"R2 Score: {r2:.4f}\")\n",
    "        print(f\"MAE: {mae:.4f}\")\n",
    "        print(f\"RMSE: {rmse:.4f}\")\n",
    "    \n",
    "    results[target] = target_results\n",
    "\n",
    "# Visualize model performance\n",
    "plt.figure(figsize=(15, 5))\n",
    "for i, target in enumerate(new_target_metrics):\n",
    "    plt.subplot(1, 3, i+1)\n",
    "    r2_scores = [results[target][model]['R2'] for model in models.keys()]\n",
    "    plt.bar(models.keys(), r2_scores)\n",
    "    plt.title(f'R2 Scores for {target}')\n",
    "    plt.xticks(rotation=45)\n",
    "    plt.ylim(0, 1)\n",
    "plt.tight_layout()\n",
    "plt.show()\n",
    "\n",
    "# Feature importance for best performing model (Random Forest)\n",
    "rf_model = RandomForestRegressor(n_estimators=100, random_state=42)\n",
    "feature_importance_dict = {}\n",
    "\n",
    "plt.figure(figsize=(12, 6))\n",
    "for i, target in enumerate(new_target_metrics):\n",
    "    rf_model.fit(X_scaled, y[:, i])\n",
    "    importance = rf_model.feature_importances_\n",
    "    feature_importance_dict[target] = dict(zip(selected_features, importance))\n",
    "    \n",
    "    plt.subplot(1, 3, i+1)\n",
    "    plt.bar(selected_features, importance)\n",
    "    plt.title(f'Feature Importance for {target}')\n",
    "    plt.xticks(rotation=90)\n",
    "plt.tight_layout()\n",
    "plt.show()\n",
    "\n",
    "print(\"\\\n",
    "Feature Importance Summary:\")\n",
    "for target, importances in feature_importance_dict.items():\n",
    "    print(f\"\\\n",
    "{target}:\")\n",
    "    sorted_features = sorted(importances.items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)\n",
    "    for feature, importance in sorted_features[:3]:\n",
    "        print(f\"{feature}: {importance:.4f}\")"
